    OneTrust.OnConsentChanged(function(e){
      var data = {}, mapKeys = {"C": "categories", "H": "hosts", "V": "vendors"},

        }
        data[key].push(item);
      }

        SA.Logger.Mone.event('gdpr', 'cookie_banner', 'consent_change', {data: data});
      }

      // For the new layout
      var event = new CustomEvent('mone-event', { detail: { type: 'gdpr', source: 'cookie_banner', action: 'consent_change', data: data} });
      window.dispatchEvent(event);
    });

baF8" data-test-id="education-cards-container"><div class="heO zA zN"><div class="qaA baN baB4"><div class="qaB zA zC zU baD3 baE8 baCQ baF5 qaC zA zM"><div class="qaE zA ba2 baBN baE baB3"><h2 class="qaF bhD baB" data-test-id="education-cards-title" id="learn-about-investing">Learn About Investing</h2></div></div></div><div class="heM"></div></div><div class="heN zA baN"><a aria-labelledby="learn-about-investing cardFooterMoreEducation" id="cardFooterMoreEducation" data-test-id="card-footer-link" class="pxA" href="/education?source=content_type%3Areact%7Cfirst_level_url%3Ahome%7Csection%3Alearn_about_investing%7Cbutton%3Amore">More Education »</a></div></section></div><div class="lbBA lbDX" data-test-id="grid-col"><section class="pzA zA zK zR fdA baDP baEU heB heA baCC heC baF8" data-test-id="about-sa-cards-container"><div class="heO zA zN"><div class="qaA baN baB4 plA plB baGI"><div class="qaB zA zC zU baD3 baE8 baCQ baF5 qaC zA zM"><div class="qaE zA ba2 baBN baE baB3"><h2 class="qaF bhD baB" data-test-id="about-sa-cards-title">About Seeking Alpha</h2></div></div></div><div class="heM"><div class="plC bfJ bfZ bfA bfBN bfCT bfD5"><p><strong>Our mission: Power to Investors.</strong> We empower investors to make the absolute best investing decisions by leveraging our independent and balanced stock research, fundamental analysis tools, crowdsourced debate, reliable news, and actionable market data.</p><p><strong>Our research</strong> is created by investors, for investors. It is carefully vetted by in-house editors, then read and debated by millions of people. Our stock coverage is wider and deeper than any other. We provide diverse opinions on each stock so that investors can weigh the bull and bear case and make an informed decision.</p><p><strong>Our news</strong> enables investors to understand why the market and the stocks in their portfolio are moving or are about to move. Investors read our financial news to gain insight into stocks’ future earnings and price trajectory, and to find new and exciting opportunities.</p><p><strong>Our data</strong> places professional-caliber tools in the hands of every investor. Our factor grades and quant ratings summarize each stock’s characteristics, and SA author ratings provide a snapshot of our contributors’ qualitative opinions.</p><p><strong>Our community</strong> includes everyone from new investors to fund managers. By helping them to invest successfully, we help them to achieve life goals such as buying their first house, sending their children to college, and securing their retirement.</p></div></div></div></section></div><div class="lbBA lbDX" data-test-id="grid-col"><section class="pzA zA zK zR fdA baDP baEU heB heA baCC heC baF8" data-test-id="become-contributor-cards-container"><div class="heO zA zN"><div class="qaA baN baB4 pmA pmB baGI"><div class="qaB zA zC zU baD3 baE8 baCQ baF5 qaC zA zM"><div class="qaE zA ba2 baBN baE baB3"><h2 class="qaF bhD baB" data-test-id="become-contributor-cards-title">Become A Contributor</h2></div></div></div><div class="heM"><div class="pmD bfJ bfZ bfA bfBN bfCT bfD5"><p>Seeking Alpha publishes research from thousands of contributors. Investors contribute articles to Seeking Alpha because they receive payment, exposure, fame, the opportunity to get feedback on their ideas, and the ability to run their own subscription research business in our Marketplace.</p><p>Our contributors include professional investors and individual investors. We believe that individual investors are often underestimated, when many individual investors have better investment track records than professionals and possess valuable insights that can help other investors.</p><p>To become a contributor you must be accepted by our editors, who ensure each author and article meets our quality and compliance standards.</p><p>To become a Seeking Alpha contributor, <a class="efC pmC" href="/submission">submit an article here.</a></p></div></div></div></section></div></div></div></div></main><div class="bwA bwB" style=""><div
